< text>
It is a good park primarily for the kids in the area to play basketball at the court and ride their bikes.  It is small as parks go and there are more relaxing parks like Heritage Lake nearby if that is your goal.  If you are looking for a spot to let the kids get some energy out this seems to be the main draw here for the nearby residents.  There are a few exercise items, benches, and a covered gazebo.  There are plaques calling it Rancho Ramona park but the biggest and most visible sign calls this John V. Denver park to help clear up any confusion finding it</text>

<Review>I had a cyst removal here last month. The procedure went well, but I was shocked when I saw the bill. Two types of charges (1. excision; 2. repair of wounds) each appeared twice on the bill, at different amounts. I thought this had to be a mistake so I called today, first their billings department and then their Mountain View office. The explanation given was that they charge for the use of Operating Room separately from physician bill. What they were unable to provide was the justification to use OR at first place.

This is the fourth cyst removal I ever had in life, so I'm definitely not new to the whole thing. The cysts I've had were always benign, and never bigger than the size of a pea. This is the first time I got billed for the use of OR, even though the procedure itself seemed just as straightforward as any of the previous ones. The doctor even commented at one point that "this is perhaps the easiest cyst removal I've even done". If they charge for the use of OR separately, they should at least justify the need to use it at first place and make sure the patient is aware of the situation.

For a 20-minutes procedure that could have easily been performed in a regular Exam Room, they billed me $2240 for the use of OR. It's about $1000 out of pocket after adjusting for insurance discount. I'll be contacting the insurance company next to see what they have to say.

<text>After my regular nail tech cancelled on me last minute, I Google searched for other shops as I was attending a special event and needed nails and pedi ASAP. <userid>100691768313216702003<//userid><username>Brian Delach</username><date>1534889465366</date><rating>5<//rating>< Review>
Habit ran a great promotion in March where they offered a free burger if you registered with their website.

I took them up on the offer since they have a location about a mile and a half from my house.

In all honesty, I was pretty blown away by the quality of the food. They make a delicious burger and I've since been back to try their strawberry & grilled chicken salad which was also excellent. I hope they'll consider making it a permanent addition to their menu.

These days, there are a lot of places you can go to get a burger, but I'll vouch for Habit being one of the better options.</Review>
